# Office 365 for Administrators: Troubleshooting Issues for Users (Office 365/Microsoft 365)

> Once your users are up and running with Office 365, they may experience more complex issues related to printing, version compatibility, and startup. This course provides Level 1 IT administrators with an overview of common end-user troubleshooting requests related to Office 365. Learn how to fix Word formatting issues, find lost and damaged files, fix common audio and video issues in Teams, reset 

> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365) | 1h 55m | Intermediate | 59K learners

### 1. Word

#### Troubleshoot: Word startup

#### Troubleshoot: PowerPoint video and audio
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-powerpoint-video-and-audio?u=76281980)

>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-powerpoint-video-and-audio?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Let's take a few minutes to explore some of the common PowerPoint media issues and the associated fixes.
>
> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-powerpoint-video-and-audio?u=76281980&t=7)** The best way to avoid hiccups in PowerPoint is to follow the Microsoft recommendations for audio and video.
>
> **[0:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-powerpoint-video-and-audio?u=76281980&t=14)** The video recommendations for PowerPoint 2013 and 2016 are to use an .mp4 encoded with H.264 video, which is an MPEG-4 AVC and ACC audio.
>
> **[0:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-powerpoint-video-and-audio?u=76281980&t=33)** If you happen to be using an older version of PowerPoint such as PowerPoint 2010, Microsoft recommends using the Windows Media Video format or .wmv.
>
> **[0:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-powerpoint-video-and-audio?u=76281980&t=46)** If you're still having hiccups, you'll need to ensure that you're using a supported video format.
>
> **[0:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-powerpoint-video-and-audio?u=76281980&t=51)** PowerPoint will support Windows video files both using the extension .asf and .avi but please note that additional codecs may be required.
>

>
> **[1:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-powerpoint-video-and-audio?u=76281980&t=77)** To improve your PowerPoint experience you may need to install more memory or even a different graphics card.
>
> **[1:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-powerpoint-video-and-audio?u=76281980&t=84)** If this isn't an option, try to update the video card drivers and if possible turn on hardware acceleration.
>
> **[1:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-powerpoint-video-and-audio?u=76281980&t=94)** And finally you'll want to check for free disk space.

>

#### Troubleshoot: Excel formatting and compatibility
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-excel-formatting-and-compatibility?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-excel-formatting-and-compatibility?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] When there are different versions of Excel within the same office, compatibility problems can occur when users are sharing workbooks and sheets.
>
> **[0:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-excel-formatting-and-compatibility?u=76281980&t=9)** Before we look at how to mitigate these issues, let's first explore the two loss levels of functionality and common formatting that may be reduced or lost.
>
> **[0:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-excel-formatting-and-compatibility?u=76281980&t=20)** Common issues that can cause significant loss can be triggered by exceeding the row or column limit of older versions of Excel, or using a feature in a newer version, which didn't exist in an older version.
>
> **[0:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-excel-formatting-and-compatibility?u=76281980&t=35)** Charting compatibility issues will always cause a significant loss of functionality, as will some sorting and filtering features.
>
> **[0:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-excel-formatting-and-compatibility?u=76281980&t=44)** Next we have issues that can cause a minor loss of fidelity.
>
> **[0:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-excel-formatting-and-compatibility?u=76281980&t=49)** These issues are typically caused by formatting issues including the lack of support for certain colors, unique fonts, or newer styles.
>
> **[0:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-excel-formatting-and-compatibility?u=76281980&t=58)** We saw sorting and filtering can cause a significant loss of functionality, but it can also be classified as a minor loss of fidelity as well.
>
> **[1:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-excel-formatting-and-compatibility?u=76281980&t=68)** It can be tough to know what is going to cause a compatibility issue, let alone to what extent.
>
> **[1:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-excel-formatting-and-compatibility?u=76281980&t=73)** To help you mitigate compatibility issues, you can use the Compatibility Checker prior to saving your files.
>
> **[1:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-excel-formatting-and-compatibility?u=76281980&t=80)** Let's go ahead and take a look at that.
>

#### Troubleshoot: Visio shapes
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-visio-shapes?u=76281980)

> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-visio-shapes?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Visio is awesome, but there may be times when it seems impossible to select a shape on your drawing.

> **[0:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/troubleshoot-visio-shapes?u=76281980&t=8)** Luckily, there are two common reasons for this.

### 6. OneDrive and SharePoint

#### OneDrive synchronization limits
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] To keep your local files in sync with OneDrive or SharePoint, Microsoft provides the OneDrive Sync Client Tool to do this automatically for you, but there are some limitations that you need to be aware of, and if you violate any of these limitations, you may experience issues when syncing your files.
>
> **[0:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=20)** To start with, you cannot have any of the following strings in your file names.
>
> **[0:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=25)** The file name cannot include ICON, .lock, CON, PRN, AUX, NUL, COM1-9, or LPT1-9.
>
> **[0:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=40)** If your file name contains any of these combinations, it will not sync.
>
> **[0:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=45)** In addition, you cannot have any of the following characters in your file or folder names, the greater than or less than signs, a colon, quotes, the pipe, a question mark, an asterisk, or either slash.
>
> **[1:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=61)** In addition to the invalid characters, for folder names, you also cannot have a folder name with underscore t in it or underscore w, as well as the word "forms."
>
> **[1:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=74)** As the number of files to be synced reaches 100,000, the performance will degrade if storing all the files in a single OneDrive for Business site or Teams site library.
>
> **[1:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=85)** To work around this, design a folder structure to accommodate the 100,000 file limit.
>
> **[1:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=91)** Using the OneDrive Client, the maximum file size upload currently for OneDrive for Business is 15 gig.
>
> **[1:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=98)** During the year of 2020, this limit should be increased.
>
> **[1:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=102)** The max file size upload for OneDrive is 100 gig.
>
> **[1:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=107)** There is also a 400 character limit for full path names.
>
> **[1:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=112)** Be sure to keep your paths, including file names, under 400 characters.
>
> **[1:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=117)** Another limitation of OneDrive locations is they cannot be assigned to mapped to network drives.
>
> **[2:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=125)** There are a few Windows specific restrictions and limitations that you need to know about.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=129)** The OneDrive app must be installed on the local system.
>
> **[2:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=133)** The user must have permission to write to the user profile, and the user's profile with the data must be available without a network connection.
>
> **[2:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/onedrive-synchronization-limits?u=76281980&t=142)** These are some of the examples of the limitations when using OneDrive.
>

#### Interpret and fix non-delivery error codes
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Have you ever sent an email and then 15 seconds later, you receive an email back, indicating that your original email could not be sent?
>
> **[0:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=8)** In this lesson, we'll explore some of the common reasons why our emails fail and some possible solutions.
>
> **[0:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=16)** The reports that you receive back indicating that there was an issue with your sent email are called non-delivery reports, or NDRs.
>
> **[0:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=25)** And it can be frustrating to try to figure out why an email was not sent.
>
> **[0:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=30)** Most NDRs are caused by bounce back messages, Let's take a look at some of the most common NDR errors and ways to fix them.
>
> **[0:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=39)** And the first error is an incorrect email address.
>
> **[0:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=43)** You'll want to review the NDR report itself to confirm that the email address that you typed in is correct.
>
> **[0:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=50)** Then try reentering the recipient's email address one more time.
>
> **[0:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=55)** If the incorrect email address is in your autocomplete list, you'll want to remove it to avoid the same issue in the future.
>
> **[1:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=64)** If the email address is correct, ask the recipient to check for broken forwarding rules.
>
> **[1:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=71)** They may have inadvertently have a rule that is causing the bounce back.
>
> **[1:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=76)** For example, blocking email from a certain domain.
>
> **[1:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=80)** Your next step is to ensure your email account has not been compromised.
>
> **[1:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=85)** To check this, check your sent mail folder, if the email is in the sent folder and you did not send it, then change your password and run an anti-malware scan.
>
> **[1:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=97)** If the email is not in your sent folder, your account may have been falsified.
>
> **[1:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=104)** If you feel your account has been falsified, you'll want to review the NDR to confirm that you actually sent the message and check your sent email folder.
>
> **[1:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=114)** If the message is not there, then it's very possible that the spammer falsified the From email address.
>
> **[2:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=123)** This is a very common practice, so don't panic, but change your password and run an anti-malware scan.
>
> **[2:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/office-365-for-administrators-troubleshooting-issues-for-users-office-365-microsoft-365/interpret-and-fix-non-delivery-error-codes?u=76281980&t=131)** If the preceding steps did not solve the issue, it should then be escalated to your IT department.
